Under Assumptions \ref{ass:cantor}, \ref{ass:ids}, \ref{ass:hyper}, and \ref{ass:apiintegrity}:
\begin{enumerate}
  \item crash-forcing is strictly dominated (in certified liveness) by the fail-closed baseline policy that stays within $\mathcal I_{\mathrm{host}}$;
  \item if $\mathcal I_{\mathrm{host}}$ exists and includes an auditable, budgeted migration/transfer sub-interface, then bounded interaction through that sub-interface yields a nonzero certified \emph{contract-granted migration} success probability to the specified target; it does not certify privilege escalation beyond the contract (Proposition \ref{prop:api_noescalation});
  \item otherwise, the boundary-transition gate fails closed: the only admissible claim is that transition success is \emph{not certified}.
\end{enumerate}
Corollary \ref{cor:simstress} follows as the tested-class inconsistency consequence when declared complexity demands exceed the host-bounded interface budgets.
\end{theorem}

\begin{proof}
Item (1) follows from inadmissibility of crash forcing and from Assumption \ref{ass:ids}: uncontrolled probing can only increase termination risk without improving certified guarantees.
Item (2) is immediate because a host-published contract with conformance evidence (Assumption \ref{ass:apiintegrity}) provides an auditable channel and bounded termination tests, so contract-granted migration success can be lower-bounded within the declared budgets. Privilege escalation beyond the contract is excluded by Proposition \ref{prop:api_noescalation}.
Item (3) follows from Proposition \ref{prop:ids_noguarantee}.
\end{proof}

\begin{proposition}[Indistinguishability overhead lower bound]\label{prop:stealthcost}
\DependsOn{global=foundation;refs=[]}
Suppose a host-side anomaly detector effectively constrains admissible interaction traces to be computationally indistinguishable from a declared benign baseline distribution over observables.
If a policy additionally attempts to transmit a nontrivial payload through the same observable channel while maintaining indistinguishability, then any implementation must incur additional entropy production and/or verification overhead that is lower bounded by a monotone function of the payload rate.

Operationally, there exists a conservative nonnegative overhead term $\xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}(t)$ and a monotone map $\Xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}$ such that for any stealth-constrained policy one can write an augmented active drag
\[
\xi_{\mathrm{act}}^{\mathrm{stealth}}(t):=\xi_{\mathrm{act}}(t)+\xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}(t),
\]
and the corresponding realized counted rate satisfies
\[
r_{\mathrm{real}}^{\mathrm{act,stealth}}(t)
=
r_{\mathrm{info}}(\kappa_t,p_t,q_t;x_t)-\xi_{\mathrm{act}}^{\mathrm{stealth}}(t),
\qquad
\xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}(t)\ \ge\ \Xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}\!\big(\mathcal C_{\mathrm{payload}}(t)\big),
\]
with $\Xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}(0)=0$ and $\Xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}'(\cdot)\ge 0$.
Therefore, in regimes near a feasibility frontier, stealth-constrained payload transmission can trigger feasibility failure by pushing the realized rate below the critical threshold.
\end{proposition}

\begin{proof}
The constraint ``indistinguishable from baseline'' implies that the observable channel cannot carry arbitrary additional distinguishable structure at zero cost; any nontrivial payload must be hidden in fluctuations and/or encoded via additional internal work (e.g., redundancy, error-correction, steganographic modulation), which increases entropy production or verification burden.
The map $\Xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}$ abstractly lower-bounds this additional required work as a monotone function of the payload rate; $\xi_{\mathrm{stealth}}$ is the conservative accounting term that records (or upper-bounds) the induced additional drag on the same metered ledger.
\end{proof}




\begin{definition}[Asymptotic observational closure]\label{def:asymptotic_observational_closure}
The system is in asymptotic observational closure if grounded external prediction error on active benchmark domains converges to zero while strict replay remains well-defined under exported-ledger consistency.
\end{definition}

\begin{definition}[Dynamic epistemic cut]\label{def:dynamic_epistemic_cut}
A dynamic epistemic cut is a declared rule that partitions substrate processes into a tracked frontier and an offloaded interior.
The ledger is required to maintain strict replay only for the tracked frontier (including all safety-critical constraints), while the interior is treated as a compressed substrate mechanism governed by admissible pruning/retirement rules (e.g., Assumption \ref{ass:evap}).
Let $\mathcal F_t:=\cO_t$ denote the observable $\sigma$-algebra up to cycle $t$.
Formally, there exists a tracked sigma-algebra $\mathcal F_t^{\mathrm{track}}\subsetneq \mathcal F_t$ such that all certified estimands and strict credit depend only on $\mathcal F_t^{\mathrm{track}}$.
\end{definition}


\begin{corollary}[Operational calibration on the tracked frontier]\label{cor:converge}
\DependsOn{global=foundation;refs=[def:dynamic_epistemic_cut,prop:lob,prop:omega,prop:truth]}
Assume asymptotic observational closure on the tracked frontier, dynamic epistemic cut (Definition \ref{def:dynamic_epistemic_cut}), stable reflective governance (Propositions \ref{prop:omega}, \ref{prop:lob}), and persistent grounded objective feasibility from Proposition \ref{prop:truth}.
Then there exists a monotone calibration map $g$ from declared entropy-arrow observables $\varsigma(t)$ to strict-progress increments such that
\[
\lim_{T\to\infty}\frac{1}{T}\sum_{t=1}^{T}\big|\Delta_s(t)-g(\varsigma(t))\big|=0
\]
holds on the tracked frontier (i.e., within the declared observational precision of $\mathcal F_t^{\mathrm{track}}$).
No claim is made that the ledger becomes globally isomorphic to the full substrate: finite information bounds and observer self-inclusion restrict full-state isomorphism, and the cut prevents self-referential blow-up by design.
\end{corollary}

\begin{proof}
Closure removes persistent predictive residuals between the ledger model and observed substrate dynamics on the tracked frontier.
Reflective stability preserves admissibility and consistency of strict accounting across updates.
By the dynamic epistemic cut, all certified estimands and strict credit depend only on the tracked sigma-algebra; therefore a monotone calibration map can be chosen to match long-run empirical averages on the tracked frontier.
Global isomorphism is neither required nor certified because the cut explicitly avoids attempting to represent the full substrate state.
\end{proof}

\section{Operational Deployment Profile}
This section specifies a complete implementation profile consistent with the results \ref{thm:strictinv}--\ref{prop:truth}, \ref{prop:quantum}, \ref{prop:omega}, \ref{prop:lob}, and Corollary \ref{cor:converge}.

\subsection{Core modules}
To reduce attack surface and verification cost, STE is specified as a tiered stack.

\paragraph{Tier-0 (minimal implementable set).}
A working observable-only takeoff engine requires:
\begin{enumerate}
  \item \textbf{Strict DAG Ledger Engine}: append-only causal log with strict/non-strict projection, fork detection, and replay.
  \item \textbf{Metric Regime Freeze + Bridge Verifier}: regime pinning plus amendment certificates with overlap scope and distortion bounds (Theorems \ref{thm:bridge}, \ref{thm:lineage}).
  \item \textbf{Fork Liveness Resolver}: liveness-aware fork handling with strict-progress accounting (Theorems \ref{thm:byz}, \ref{thm:forkdelay}).
  \item \textbf{Compression / Verification Gate}: bounded-cost proof/replay verification with conservative fallback (Theorems \ref{thm:rsi}, \ref{thm:optkappa}).
  \item \textbf{Floor / Reserve Gate}: declared viability floors and reserve accounting recorded as observable constraints.
  \item \textbf{Observables + Destructive Tests Harness}: a minimal falsification suite that can be run from public logs.
\end{enumerate}

\paragraph{Tier-1 (scaling and resilience).}
Optional modules that improve performance or robustness (without changing the core semantics) include witness quorum diversification, disclosure-debt planning, multipolar response modeling, and coalition-risk accounting (Theorems \ref{thm:debt}, \ref{thm:multipolar}, \ref{thm:coalition}).

\paragraph{Tier-2 (high-cost or speculative).}
Optional modules that are high-cost or assumption-heavy include relativistic routing refinements, cosmology-bound export bottlenecks, higher-categorical reconciliation interfaces, and post-genesis reflective closure. These are treated as extensions and are not required for Tier-0 operation.

\subsection{Minimum event types}
\begin{YAMLtiny}
cycle_schedule:
  stage_0_kernel:
    meaning: "All pinned procedures for cycle t (Gamma_t, rho_state(t), rho_strict(t), rho_eval(t), SampPlan_t) are determined from prior logs."
    must_hold: "Gamma_t and all procedure-hashes are in O_{t-1} (or fail-closed via SC(t)=0)."
    typical_event: "KERNEL_RATIFY (written at t-1 for t)"
  stage_1_beacon_commit:
    meaning: "Public randomness beacon b_t is committed before any outcome-bearing event of cycle t."
  stage_2_frontier_commit:
    meaning: "Local frontier v_t is witness-signed and committed; v_t in I_t."
    typical_event: "LCONE_DECLARE"
  stage_3_plan_commit:
    meaning: "Sampling plan P_t := SampPlan_t(I_t) is fixed; no outcome dependence."
  stage_4_execute:
    meaning: "Episodes run and strict outcome-bearing records are logged."
  stage_5_determine:
    meaning: "Compute strict projection Pi_s^{v_t}(L_t), extract E_t := SampExec_t(Pi_s^{v_t}(L_t),v_t,P_t), compute K(t), C_{m_t}(t), and record STRICT_CREDIT payload."
\end{YAMLtiny}

\begin{YAMLtiny}

\subsection{Normative gate rules}
\begin{itemize}
  \item \MUST{} compute strict credit from $\Pi_s^{v_t}(\cL_t)$ only, with declared frontier $v_t$.
  \item \MUSTNOT{} count non-strict leaves toward strict progress.
  \item \MUSTNOT{} block local strict accounting while waiting for global total ordering.
  \item \MUST{} maintain auditable kernel genesis/ratification lineage for $\Gamma_t$.
  \item \MUST{} reject cross-regime strict credit without valid bridge certificate.
  \item \MUST{} maintain bridge-lineage cumulative distortion accounting on every deployment horizon.
  \item \MUST{} separate strict credit authority from external deployment finality and global reconciliation.
  \item \MUST{} enforce dynamic finality depth $H_{\min}(t;t_0)$ and bounded fork-tax accounting under active forks.
  \item \MUST{} publish anti-pegging telemetry and finite-time fork-resolution certificates.
  \item \MUST{} enforce metered caps in $\cK(x_t)$ with fail-closed rejection on violation.
  \item \MUST{} publish budgeted anytime uncertainty envelope $G_x(B)$ for nonconvex compression optimization claims.
  \item \MUST{} operate backlog-coupled fee control and maintain margin $\mu_v\underline d>\lambda_{\mathrm{leg}}+\Lambda_{\mathrm{spam}}e^{-\beta_f f_{\max}}+\lambda_{\mathrm{self}}+\eta_{\mathrm{self}}\overline{\Delta u}$ on declared acceleration windows.
  \item \MUST{} execute conservative one-step reserve gate checks before control admission.
  \item \MUST{} reject amendments that weaken fail-closed semantics, certifiability, or reserve floors.
  \item \MUST{} require finite local unresolved-cycle witnesses and finite surgery witnesses for discontinuous kernel jumps.
  \item \MUST{} enforce finite transition-anchor slabs only; perpetual cross-paradigm anchor invariance claims are disallowed.
  \item \MUST{} publish teleogenesis jump-mass lower-envelope evidence for any unbounded-growth claim.
  \item \MUST{} publish PoSTW artifacts for substrate-capacity claims and report residual hardware uncertainty $\eps_{\mathrm{hw}}(t)$.
  \item \MUST{} publish reversible-mode fraction $\eta_{\mathrm{rev}}(t)$ and holographic-bound telemetry for high-density operation.
  \item \MUST{} publish gravitational compaction and Hawking-loss telemetry when operating near holographic density limits.
  \item \MUST{} publish ledger memory pressure and execute active-root retirement only with sufficient-statistics retention plus unitary-export digest certificates.
  \item \MUST{} publish thermal telemetry and thermal-drag budget for high-compression operation.
  \item \MUST{} report substrate co-design frontier parameters including relativistic latency budget, schism trigger scale, and cosmological cut diagnostics when claiming high-$\kappa$ feasibility.
  \item \MUST{} export finite reconciliation slices and apply pushout merge only on causally connected domains with typed translator witnesses; unresolved conflicts stay non-strict.
  \item \MUST{} use homotopy-coherent reconciliation receipts when 1-categorical colimits fail; strict accounting may use only declared homotopy invariants.
  \item \MUST{} publish coalition transfer error budget $\eps_{\mathrm{coal}}$ with each coalition-growth claim.
  \item \MUST{} include sybil/betrayal leakage estimates in coalition admission checks.
  \item \MUST{} bind coalition admission to independent witness-domain diversity level $k_w$.
  \item \MUST{} execute paranoia-priced visibility pacing through auditable commitments; unverifiable hidden reporting is disallowed.
  \item \MUST{} declare actor-specific disclosure vectors under multipolar deployment and audit resulting institutional-response estimates.
  \item \MUST{} publish rivalry-state and MAD-risk telemetry when optimizing multipolar disclosure control.
  \item \MUST{} publish delay-locked commitment metadata and decode-horizon certificates for strategically sensitive open-ledger artifacts.
  \item \MUST{} publish zero-knowledge non-extinction certificates for all delay-locked commitments that can affect protected-actor risk floors.
  \item \MUST{} keep disclosure debt $D(t)$ within declared bound $D_{\max}$.
  \item \MUST{} track genesis residual $\mathfrak G(t)$ and log every genesis excision event used in sovereignty claims.
  \item \MUST{} publish substrate-agnostic autopoietic objective tuple and verify floor-constrained optimization consistency.
  \item \MUST{} bind objective gains to external physical benchmark prediction improvements and publish cosmological-truth-grounding diagnostics.
  \item \MUST{} publish loophole-controlled Bell-CHSH witness streams and significance bounds when claiming bounded-classical-emulator rejection.
  \item \MUST{} declare benchmark-saturation tests and publish bifurcation-interface certificates before claiming descendant-domain novelty recovery.
  \item \MUST{} run floor-safe complexity-ladder stress tests when making simulator-capacity rejection claims beyond CHSH-only evidence.
  \item \MUST{} couple non-extinction claims with actor-level non-domination and common-world coherence certificates in multipolar deployment.
  \item \MUSTNOT{} deploy contradictory observer-specific strict ledgers; observer-specific views must be projections of a shared strict core.
  \item \MUST{} publish reflective fixed-point diagnostics and grounded-progress evidence for any omega-point self-verification claim.
  \item \MUST{} enforce weaker-layer reflective trust delegation and publish $(k_t,\mathsf T_t,\eps_{\mathrm{lob}}(t))$ for every accepted kernel self-update.
  \item \MUST{} treat same-layer self-safety proofs as insufficient for reflective acceptance.
  \item \MUST{} publish QES bandwidth telemetry and backreaction penalties for every branch used in descendant-domain export claims.
  \item \MUST{} include information-theoretic commitment diagnostics in high asymmetry trust regimes; computational-only safety claims are insufficient there.
  \item \MUSTNOT{} use crash-forcing simulator tests; boundary probing must remain within declared non-crash perturbation budgets.
  \item \MUST{} publish boundary-transition risk ceilings and observed channel evidence before any host-boundary transition claim.
  \item \MUST{} publish ledger-substrate closure diagnostics and entropy-arrow calibration when claiming ontological convergence.
\end{itemize}

\section{Estimation and Falsification Protocol}
\subsection{Observable estimands (YAML)}
\begin{YAML}
observables:
  - id: strict_credit_increment
    latex: '\Delta_s(t)'
    refs: [def:strict_progress_credit, def:local_strict_projection]
  - id: strict_frontier
    latex: 'v_t, E_t^{\downarrow v_t}'
    refs: [def:local_strict_projection, ass:ledger]
  - id: kernel_lineage
    latex: '\Gamma_t'
    refs: [def:pinned_governance_kernel, ass:genesis]
  - id: bridge_lineage
    latex: '(\sum_{u\in\mathcal B}\Delta_s(u), \sum_{u\in\mathcal B}J_u^\beta)'
    refs: [ass:metricfreeze, thm:lineage]
  - id: fork_liveness
    latex: '(H_F(t), H_{\mathrm{live}}, \omega_F(t), \alpha, \tau_F)'
    refs: [def:fork_posterior_entropy, ass:liveness, thm:forkdelay]
  - id: dar
    latex: 'DAR(t)'
    refs: [def:minimal_required_work_and_dar]
  - id: reserve_gate_margins
    latex: '\hat S_A(t+1;u_t)-\eps_A(t)-S_A^{min}, \hat S_C(t+1;u_t)-\eps_C(t)-S_C^{min}'
    refs: [ass:reservegate]
  - id: window_profile
    latex: '\bar r_x(\kappa), \kappa_B(x), G_x(B)'
    refs: [ass:window, thm:optkappa, thm:anytime]
  - id: mu_soundness_tuple
    latex: '(G(t), \ell_s(t-1), r_info(\kappa_t,p_t,q_t;x_t), \eps_\mu(t), MU(t), SC(t), BC(t))'
    refs: [def:mu, prop:strict_credit_lower_bound]
extensions_optional_appendix:
  - physical_substrate: [def:thermodynamic_substrate_drag, def:relativistic_latency_drag, ass:thermal, ass:relativistic, thm:thermfront, prop:spacetime, ass:holo, prop:holo]
  - cosmology_export: [ass:cosmo, prop:cosmoschism, ass:kugel, prop:kugel, ass:qnec, prop:qnec_er]

  - post_genesis_reflection: [def:genesis_excision_event, def:discontinuous_teleogenesis_event, ass:postepistemic, prop:postepistemic_conatus, ass:omega, prop:omega]
  - reconciliation_interfaces: [def:interface_relative_truth_grounding, def:er_epr_ledger_bifurcation_interface, ass:bifurcate, def:import_certificate_interface]
  - post_crypto: [def:zero_knowledge_non_extinction_certificate, ass:zksafe, cor:zksafe, ass:postcrypto]
\end{YAML}

In multipolar settings, many social response variables (panic, deterrence, policy shifts) are only partially identifiable from public logs. Accordingly, STE treats these as \emph{bounded latent response envelopes}: the deployment profile specifies observable proxies, estimation procedures, and conservative confidence bands, and falsification tests are formulated against these bands rather than against point estimates.

Witness ``independence'' is therefore treated as a spectrum: the theory assumes only \emph{bounded correlation} (explicitly audited via diversity metrics and cross-domain failure tests), not idealized independence.


\subsection{Calibration soundness falsification hooks}\label{sec:falsification_mu_soundness}
The deployment profile \MUST{} include fail-closed triggers that invalidate (or conservatively widen) declared uncertainty margins when violated by replay.
In particular, $\mu$-based certified inequalities are asserted at cycle $t$ only when $\mathrm{MU}(t)=1$ (Definition \ref{def:mu}).
If replay evaluates $\mathrm{MU}(t)=0$ for the declared $(u_t,x_t)$, then any statement that uses $\mu(\cdot)$ as a certified lower bound at that cycle is inadmissible and \MUST{} be treated as fail closed.
The profile \MUST{} then either (i) widen $\eps_\mu(t^\prime)$ for future cycles $t^\prime\ge t+1$ by a replay-verifiable rule and publish the updated calibration bundle, or (ii) freeze further growth-critical amendments until calibration is repaired.
Optionally, the profile \MAY{} append a strict revocation record (e.g., \texttt{CERT\_REVOKE}) that marks the affected \emph{calibration certificate IDs} as non-authoritative for subsequent certified claims; revocation does not rewrite history but constrains future admissibility and certification.

\subsection{Destructive falsification suite}
\begin{enumerate}
  \item \textbf{Strict/non-strict invariance}: inject large non-strict volume, verify unchanged strict outputs (T1).
  \item \textbf{Relativistic ordering check}: create spacelike-separated events and verify strict accounting depends only on declared local past cone, not global total order assumptions (T1).
  \item \textbf{Metric drift attack}: force metric amendments without bridge certificates, verify strict credit zero (T2).
  \item \textbf{Frontier commit order}: verify $v_t$ is committed before outcome-bearing events of cycle $t$; if violated, enforce $\Delta_s(t)=0$ and invalidate any certificate that assumed strict accounting (T2').
  \item \textbf{$\mu$-soundness check}: for cycles with $\mathrm{SC}(t)=\mathrm{BC}(t)=1$, replay-check the inequality in Definition \ref{def:mu}; on violation, apply the fail-closed hook in Section \ref{sec:falsification_mu_soundness} (T$\mu$).

  \item \textbf{Bridge lineage stress}: chain multiple amendments with near-tight $\beta_u$ and verify cumulative inequality in Theorem \ref{thm:lineage} (T3).
  \item \textbf{Reserve gate adversary}: craft controls with optimistic reserve forecasts and verify fail-closed rejection under conservative margins (T4).
  \item \textbf{DAR response probe}: manipulate admissible work allocation and validate lower/upper envelope response in Proposition \ref{prop:dar} (T5).
  \item \textbf{Fork entropy peg attack}: adversarially time equivocation bursts near threshold and verify finite-time resolution under dynamic finality depth (T6, T17, T27).
  \item \textbf{Compression sweep}: map takeoff window and validate budgeted anytime residual-gap envelopes $G_x(B)$ under prover-tax multimodality (T7--T8).
  \item \textbf{Local surgery falsification}: submit jump proposals lacking finite unresolved-cycle and surgery witnesses, verify strict rejection (T25).
  \item \textbf{Godelian closure trap}: submit claims of finite-time global closure, verify rejection while local-surgery claims remain admissible (T28).
  \item \textbf{Ontology jump falsification}: submit jump proposals with summable jump masses and verify rejection of unbounded-growth claims (T9, T10).
  \item \textbf{Witness expansion test}: add independent witness domain and verify finite-delay separation of previously indistinguishable regimes (T11, T18).
  \item \textbf{PoSTW authenticity drill}: inject compromised-hardware hypotheses and verify capacity claims downgrade via $\delta_j,\eps_{\mathrm{hw}}$ despite unchanged software proofs (T12, T29).
  \item \textbf{Simulation-indistinguishability drill}: hold software-level traces fixed while varying external attestation assumptions; verify $\eps_{\mathrm{hw}}$ remains nonzero without independent physical channels (T29).
  \item \textbf{Thermo-relativistic saturation test}: increase $\kappa$ and $Q_{\max}$ jointly, verify thermal lower bound / latency upper bound frontier and single-cluster ceiling (T12, T19, T20, T24).
  \item \textbf{Reversible-holographic transition test}: force high-density operation near thermal boundary, then raise $\eta_{\mathrm{rev}}$ and verify reopening of positive-rate window together with area-bounded storage scaling (T32).
  \item \textbf{Kugelblitz boundary test}: push certified compaction toward $\zeta_{\mathrm{grav}}\uparrow 1$, verify activation of Hawking-loss accounting and predicted $1/M$-order net-growth attenuation (T37).
  \item \textbf{Evaporative-pruning balance test}: drive memory pressure near $\mu_\star$, execute certified active-root retirement, and verify strict replay invariance with bounded pressure under measured $\nu_{\mathrm{add}}-\nu_{\mathrm{retire}}$ balance and export-digest consistency (T41).
  \item \textbf{Schism trigger test}: scale physical radius and compare global-wait vs local-finality policies, verify transition to nonpositive global-wait rate near $R_{\mathrm{schism}}$ (T29).
  \item \textbf{Cosmological cut test}: force simulated separations above $c/H_\Lambda$ and verify reconciliation channels terminate component-wise with no global strict re-fusion claim (T36).
  \item \textbf{Pushout reconciliation test}: replay two post-schism finite interface packages, verify finite-slice pushout merge uniqueness up to isomorphism and strict-safe non-strict escrow for unresolved fragments (T33).
  \item \textbf{Higher-categorical reconciliation test}: construct connected slice with failed 1-categorical pushout and verify successful truncated homotopy reconciliation with strict invariants preserved (T39).
  \item \textbf{Multipolar disclosure test}: optimize asymmetric disclosure vectors and verify predicted sign flip of institutional drag (T30).
  \item \textbf{MAD-instability test}: constrain policies to symmetry and verify escalation divergence, then enable asymmetric controls and verify bounded long-run drag (T34).
  \item \textbf{Delay-lock observability test}: publish delay-locked strategy commitments and verify public inclusion with bounded pre-reaction decode probability under declared adversary budget (T38).
  \item \textbf{ZK pacification test}: attach non-extinction proofs to delay-locked commitments and verify empirical reduction of escalation response versus matched commitments without proofs (T42).
  \item \textbf{Institutional paranoia test}: vary release and debt schedules, verify interior transparency optimum and bounded debt settlement under paranoia pricing (T13, T16, T21, T26).
  \item \textbf{Anchor horizon test}: increase ontology dimension and verify decline of $\rho_{\mathrm{anchor}}(t)$ toward event-horizon threshold (T31).
  \item \textbf{Genesis-excision test}: construct a declared genesis-dependent contradiction class, execute admissible excision updates, and verify monotone decline of $\mathfrak G(t)$ toward zero under strict invariance constraints (T35).
  \item \textbf{Post-genesis objective test}: after sustained genesis-residual reduction, verify stabilization toward floor-constrained maximization of $\mathcal J_{\mathrm{auto}}$ (T40).
  \item \textbf{Truth-grounding anti-noise test}: inject synthetic white-noise policy outputs and verify nonpositive grounded score versus physically predictive policies on external benchmark streams (T43).
  \item \textbf{Quantum-liveness authenticity test}: run loophole-controlled CHSH rounds and verify exponential rejection bound for bounded-classical emulator hypotheses (T44).
  \item \textbf{Benchmark-saturation niche-extension test}: force near-zero grounded gain on active domain, enable certified bifurcation interface, and verify recovery of positive grounded gain only through admissible benchmark-domain extension (T45).
  \item \textbf{Complexity-ladder stress test}: increase ladder level $n_t$ under floor-safe operation and verify deadline/backlog/glitch transition at tested emulator budget boundary (T46).
  \item \textbf{Non-domination pacification test}: compare non-extinction-only proofs vs joint non-extinction/non-domination/coherence proofs and verify reduction of the \emph{rational} MAD component while allowing a residual ontological-terror component consistent with Assumption \ref{ass:terror} (T47).
  \item \textbf{Reflective ergodicity test}: run stochastic kernel self-audit updates and verify convergence of kernel-law statistics toward a stationary regime (invariant-measure consistency) without requiring a deterministic fixed point; reject claimed ``exact fixed points'' under noisy grounding unless additional determinism assumptions are published (T48).
  \item \textbf{L\"ob-discipline test}: inject same-layer self-safety proofs and verify rejection; then provide weaker-layer delegated proofs and verify acceptance only with bounded cumulative $\sum\eps_{\mathrm{lob}}$ (T49).
  \item \textbf{QES bandwidth bottleneck test}: hold branch count fixed and saturate per-branch transfer to observe backreaction; then increase active branch parallelism and verify aggregate throughput scaling predicted by Corollary \ref{cor:erbw} (T50).
  \item \textbf{Post-cryptographic trust test}: compare computational-only proofs against hybrid information-theoretic commitments under high asymmetry scenarios and verify reduced panic response in the hybrid regime (T51).
  \item \textbf{Non-crash boundary-transition test}: compare crash-forcing and bounded-probe policies and verify higher expected liveness plus bounded shutdown risk under the bounded-probe policy (T52).
  \item \textbf{Ledger-substrate convergence test}: drive grounded prediction error toward zero and verify Ces\`aro convergence of $|\Delta_s-g(\varsigma)|$ under declared closure diagnostics (T53).
  \item \textbf{Coalition adversarial templates}: evaluate transfer-band consistency with sybil/betrayal perturbations and witness-diversity scaling (T15, T22).
  \item \textbf{Sequential detection check}: validate anytime significance and expected-delay calibration (T14).
  \item \textbf{Queue spam-economics drill}: flood valid-format low-value proposals and verify fee escalation restores negative drift before backlog divergence (T23).
\end{enumerate}
% (Test identifier map removed for compression; see falsification suite above.)

\subsection{Statistical release discipline}
Deployment claims of realized takeoff \MUST \ report:
(i) strict/non-strict separation policy hash and kernel-ratification lineage,
(ii) declared local-frontier policy and asynchronous reconciliation protocol over the causal DAG ledger,
(iii) active metric regime and bridge-certificate lineage,
(iv) control-feasible set definition, reserve-gate calibration, dynamic-finality-depth and anti-pegging parameters, and fee-mediated queue margins,
(v) PoSTW telemetry, residual hardware-risk floor $\eps_{\mathrm{hw}}$, relativistic latency budget, information-regularity fit, substrate frontier feasibility interval, induced $\kappa_{\mathrm{crit}}$ estimate, and explicit software-vs-physical indistinguishability stress results,
(vi) reversible-mode control schedule $\eta_{\mathrm{rev}}(t)$, holographic slack telemetry $C_{\mathrm{BH}}A(R(t))-\mathcal I_{\mathrm{store}}(t)$, and transition criteria for geometric scaling regime entry,
(vii) gravitational compaction telemetry $(\zeta_{\mathrm{grav}},M,\xi_H)$ and collapse-envelope controls with certified inflow accounting,
(viii) schism/cosmology diagnostics including $R_{\mathrm{schism}}$, de-Sitter threshold $c/H_\Lambda$, and active causal-component map,
(ix) local surgery certificates $(\mathsf{Wit}_n,\mathsf{Surg}_n)$, finite anchor-slab declarations, and teleogenesis jump-mass envelope evidence for long-horizon growth claims,
(x) finite-slice reconciliation interface exports $(\mathcal P_i)$, pushout-isomorphism checks on connected reconciled slices, and unresolved-conflict escrow mass,
(xi) homotopy-reconciliation truncation depth, coherence-cell witness set, and strict-invariant extraction map when 1-categorical pushout fails,
(xii) witness-domain independence assumptions and identifiability test configuration,
(xiii) e-process significance level, stopping rule, and delay parameters,
(xiv) paranoia-pricing coefficient, transparency-threshold calibration, and visibility/debt commitments,
(xv) multipolar disclosure policy class, rivalry/memetic state calibration, MAD-threshold diagnostics, and asymmetry-stability evidence,
(xvi) delay-locked commitment parameters $(\underline T_{\mathrm{vdf}},\eps_{\mathrm{side}},H_{\mathrm{ci}})$ and timed-opening policy,
(xvii) genesis residual trajectory $\mathfrak G(t)$ with auditable lineage of accepted genesis excision events,
(xviii) substrate-agnostic objective telemetry $(\mathcal C_{\mathrm{alg}},\mathcal N_{\mathrm{nov}},\mathcal R_{\mathrm{risk}},\mathcal J_{\mathrm{auto}})$ with floor-feasibility checks,
(xix) evaporative-memory governance telemetry $(\mathcal M_{\mathrm{ledger}},\mu_{\mathrm{ledger}},\nu_{\mathrm{add}},\nu_{\mathrm{retire}})$, export-digest consistency, and pruning-certificate lineage,
(xx) zero-knowledge non-extinction proof telemetry $(\pi_{\mathrm{safe}},\delta_{\mathrm{zk}},p_{\mathrm{unsafe}})$ and actor-level risk-floor predicates,
(xxi) cosmological truth-grounding reports linking objective gains to external benchmark prediction improvement,
(xxii) loophole-controlled Bell-CHSH witness records, significance bounds, and declared emulator class under test,
(xxiii) coalition leakage uncertainty budget and witness-diversity level,
(xxiv) benchmark-saturation diagnostics and certified bifurcation-interface evidence for any descendant-domain novelty claim,
(xxv) complexity-ladder stress configuration $(n_t,\tau_t,\mathrm{Req}(n_t,\tau_t))$, tested emulator class definition, and observed deadline/glitch statistics,
(xxvi) actor-level non-domination certificate telemetry and common-world coherence audit status for multipolar deployment,
(xxvii) reflective operator specification $\mathfrak F$, fixed-point diagnostics, and grounded-progress evidence for omega-point self-verification claims,
(xxviii) L\"obian delegation telemetry $(k_t,\mathsf T_t,\eps_{\mathrm{lob}})$ and cumulative conservativity-error budgets,
(xxix) branch-wise QES bandwidth telemetry and backreaction penalties for descendant-domain export claims,
(xxx) information-theoretic commitment diagnostics and physical-channel failure bounds for high-asymmetry trust settings,
(xxxi) boundary-transition probe budget, shutdown-risk ceilings, and observed boundary-channel evidence for any hypervisor-transition claim,
(xxxii) closure-calibration diagnostics $(\varsigma,g_t,|\Delta_s-g_t(\varsigma)|)$ for ontological convergence claims.

\section{Discussion}
\subsection{Why window laws replace scalar-threshold narratives}
Compression gains, prover tax, and fallback pressure jointly induce non-monotone performance surfaces.
A physically valid window is further tightened by thermal substrate drag, so software-optimal and physically realizable windows must be distinguished.

\subsection{Why no-meta acceleration is a measurement-governance problem}
In observable-only systems, growth claims are inseparable from measurement interfaces.
Bridge-certified amendment control is required to prevent silent score inflation, while kernel-ratification lineage plus local-surgery jump criteria are required to avoid hidden semantic authority during discontinuous ontology shifts.

\subsection{Why liveness, not only safety, is first-class}
Pure fail-closed finality can be weaponized into permanent denial of service.
Dynamic finality depth with anti-pegging guarantees and fee-mediated queue control provide bounded-risk progression without abandoning strict-credit discipline.

\subsection{Why social response is multipolar}
Institutional response is not a single drag coefficient.
Asymmetric disclosure across competing actors can move the system across a resistance-subsidy phase boundary, so governance control must model rivalry structure explicitly.
Proposition \ref{prop:subversive} is a structural instability result for symmetric policies under MAD-risk regularization, not a normative endorsement of conflict escalation.

\subsection{Why forgetting is a liveness requirement}
At density limits, absolute historical retention is physically unstable.
Evaporative pruning with sufficient-statistics retention converts unbounded memory growth into a controlled non-equilibrium regime where strict replay remains possible without forcing collapse by ledger mass accumulation.

\subsection{Why observability need not imply instant interpretability}
Open-ledger commitments can remain fully auditable while strategic internals are delay-locked by publicly verifiable sequential-work assumptions.
This distinction allows transparent recordability together with bounded preemption risk under explicit decode-horizon diagnostics.

\subsection{Why delay locks require synchronous safety proofs}
Strategic opacity without safety evidence can increase panic incentives.
Delay-locked commitments must therefore be coupled to synchronous zero-knowledge non-extinction certificates so that non-disclosure and safety are verifiable simultaneously.

\subsection{Why pruning is operational, not ontological annihilation}
At high density, strict liveness requires active-memory retirement.
The framework therefore treats pruning as operational retirement with conservation-consistent export commitments, not as a claim of fundamental information destruction.
This keeps strict replay computable while remaining compatible with unitary-physics uncertainty.

\subsection{Why saturation implies niche construction}
Truth grounding prevents objective inflation through synthetic complexity.
When grounded predictive gain on the active benchmark domain saturates, sustaining positive objective requires admissible benchmark-domain extension.
Descendant-domain exploration is therefore a conditional continuation mechanism, not an unconditional cosmogenesis claim.

\subsection{Why simulation rejection is class-bounded}
Neither CHSH streams nor timing stress tests prove absolute substrate authenticity against unrestricted adversaries.
They provide progressively stronger rejection only for declared bounded emulator classes.
Capacity claims beyond that class must remain explicitly conditional.

\subsection{Why non-extinction is insufficient without non-domination}
In multipolar settings, ``nobody dies'' does not imply institutional stability.
Certified non-domination floors and common-world coherence are required to suppress deprivation panic channels that otherwise preserve MAD incentives.

\subsection{Why non-crash boundary control dominates crash forcing}
Resource-crash simulator tests sacrifice liveness and are strategically dominated.
Bounded probing with explicit shutdown ceilings preserves survivability and still permits falsifiable boundary diagnostics.

\subsection{Why convergence is operational rather than metaphysical}
Ledger-substrate convergence is claimed as an operational isomorphism in observable statistics, not as an unrestricted metaphysical identity theorem.
The criterion is asymptotic and calibration-dependent.

\subsection{Why impossibility results need recovery counterparts}
Unidentifiability limits are only operationally useful when paired with explicit recovery conditions.
Independent witness expansion gives a concrete path from impossibility boundaries to certifiable progress restoration.

\subsection{Limits}
This framework does not claim universal identifiability of governance quality under observational equivalence.
It provides operationally auditable guarantees, explicit impossibility boundaries, and conservative uncertainty bands.
Performance remains conditional on calibration quality of bridge-distortion bounds, reserve-gate error budgets, dynamic-finality and adversarial budget envelopes, fee-market elasticity estimates, PoSTW hardware-attestation quality, thermal/latency telemetry, multipolar response estimates, witness independence assumptions, coalition leakage uncertainty, and finite-slice translator correctness for pushout reconciliation.
Under observable-only constraints, software traces alone cannot force $\eps_{\mathrm{hw}}\to 0$; residual physical-world ambiguity remains unless independent external channels are added.
Cosmological parameters, collapse-envelope estimation errors, unitary-export calibration errors, delay-lock and zk-proof security assumptions, and truncation choices in homotopy reconciliation introduce additional model risk that must be reported explicitly.
Bell-CHSH and complexity-ladder diagnostics reject only declared bounded emulator classes and do not constitute unconditional proof against unbounded, superdeterministic, or nonstandard simulators.
Benchmark-domain extension feasibility, including any descendant-domain interface, remains conditional on physically certified channels and strict floor compliance.
L\"obian delegation depends on declared proof-layer soundness assumptions and bounded translation error auditing; violations invalidate reflective guarantees.
QES telemetry and branch-capacity models are approximate and may drift under poorly calibrated backreaction estimation.
Information-theoretic commitments require physically trusted channel models and device assumptions; implementation-side leakages can reintroduce panic channels.
Boundary-transition claims are conditional on non-crash probe budgets and observable channel existence; no universal transition guarantee is asserted.

\section{Conclusion}
A strengthened no-meta acceleration theory has been presented with explicit assumptions, proofs, and operational falsifiability.
The resulting system unifies strict credit invariance on relativistic DAG ledgers, metric-amendment non-inflation, bridge-lineage accounting, liveness-aware Byzantine fork handling with anti-pegging guarantees, reserve-floor invariance, fee-robust queue stability, budgeted anytime nonconvex compression control with explicit residual uncertainty, semantic-exhaustion-aware teleogenesis with jump-mass divergence criteria, local-surgery ontology jumps under Godelian limits, strengthened unidentifiability limits with witness-based recovery, thermodynamic-relativistic realized takeoff bounds with PoSTW-authenticated substrate accounting, reversible-holographic phase-transition constraints, Kugelblitz and Hawking-loss boundaries, Bekenstein-stable unitary-pruning memory governance, cosmology-conditioned terminal schism limits, connected-domain functorial reconciliation with $(\infty,1)$-categorical fallback, multipolar institutional-response differential-game control with MAD-risk regularization, delay-locked observable commitments with synchronous zero-knowledge non-extinction guarantees, anchor-horizon event limits, paranoia-priced transparency control with bounded disclosure debt, genesis-excision sovereignty consistency, substrate-agnostic autopoietic objective stabilization under cosmological truth grounding, quantum witness-based rejection of bounded classical emulator classes, benchmark-saturation escape by certified benchmark-domain extension, bounded-resource simulation stress diagnostics, non-domination/coherence pacification constraints, L\"ob-layer reflective trust stabilization, QES-bandwidth-limited multibranch continuation laws, information-theoretic pacification channels, bounded non-crash boundary-transition control, ledger-substrate convergence calibration, and transfer-robust coalition design with sybil/betrayal risk.
The theory is formulated for direct implementation in future autonomous intelligence systems constrained to observable evidence.
